msg:The hotel is in a good location, just a few minutes' walk to the beach, and next to the Kingdom of Discovery. Parking is convenient, and there are sufficient Weilai charging stations.

We chose to travel off-peak. Manager Cao Yang contacted us enthusiastically before check-in to understand the details of the itinerary and room type preferences, carefully arranged a suitable room and upgraded the room type. He also kept in touch after check-in, which was considerate and thoughtful. We decided to continue staying.

The front desk and reception staff were enthusiastic and meticulous, the room service responded promptly, and the buffet breakfast was rich in variety.

Hot springs are naturally the highlight here. There are various outdoor pools with different health functions and different appearance styles. The overall area is large and does not interfere with each other. It is very pleasant to soak and count stars at night. The indoor area is divided into several areas. The constant temperature parent-child hall is like coming to the tropics. The water slide in the paddling pool is very suitable for children to release their energy. In addition to the regular hot spring pool, the living water hall also has a large swimming pool and a large massage hot spring pool. There is a Dead Sea floating on the second floor of the ocean therapy center, which is charged but worth experiencing. There are also multiple seawater pools, and the area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe first floor is particularly large. There is a children's playground. In addition to the guests here, there are also guests from nearby hotels who come to soak in hot springs.

The enthusiasm of our Northeast friends can be felt everywhere, which is also the most impressive part of this trip. I will choose to stay here again next time I come to Jin****an.
